And while some people may seem content with the story as it stands, our view is that there exists countless mysteries, scientific anomalies and surprising artifacts that&nbsp;have yet to be discovered and explained.</p><p>The&nbsp;goal of Ancient Origins is to highlight recent archaeological discoveries, peer-reviewed academic research and evidence, as well as offering alternative viewpoints and explanations of science, archaeology, mythology, religion and history around the globe.</p><p>Were the&nbsp;only&nbsp;Pop Archaeology site combining scientific research with out-of-the-box perspectives.</p><p>By bringing together top experts and authors, this archaeology website explores lost civilizations, examines sacred writings, tours ancient places, investigates ancient discoveries and questions mysterious happenings. Our open community is dedicated to digging into the origins of our species on planet earth, and question wherever the discoveries might take us. We seek to retell the story of our beginnings.&nbsp;</p> </div>\n</div></div> </div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"grid_4\"> <div class=\"region region-postscript-2\">\n<div id=\"block-views-galleries-block-2\" class=\"block block-views\"><div class=\"block-inner\">\n<h3 class=\"title\"><span>Ancient Image Galleries</span></h3>\n<div class=\"content\">\n<div class=\"view view-galleries view-id-galleries view-display-id-block_2 view-dom-id-4cb879e83e522fec212019bffddd2f0b\">\n<div class=\"view-content\">\n<table class=\"views-view-grid cols-1\">\n<tbody>\n<tr class=\"row-1 row-first\">\n<td class=\"col-1 col-first\">\n<div class=\"views-field views-field-field-photogal\"> <div class=\"field-content galleries-image\"><a href=\"/rothenburg-ob-der-tauber-germany-006555\"><span><img typeof=\"foaf:Image\" src=\"http://www.ancient-origins.net/sites/default/files/styles/thumbnail/public/Castle-Gate-view.jpg?itok=EB3ll5Wv\" width=\"270\" height=\"120\" alt=\"View from the Castle Gate (Burgtor).
